				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					O ewiges Feuer, o Ursprung der Liebe, BWV 34 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1726-27 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">O ewiges Feuer, o Ursprung der Liebe [I]
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">O eternal fire, o source of love [I]
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="fr, de, nl">O ewiges Feuer, o Ursprung der Liebe</span>; <span title="it">O ewiges Feuer, o Ursprung der Liebe BWV 34</span>; <span title="ca, es">O ewiges Feuer</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/218100872">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/O_ewiges_Feuer,_o_Ursprung_der_Liebe,_BWV_34">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/218100872">218100872</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb148076682">148076682</a>
</td></tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>

<td>BWV 34&#160;; BC A84
</td></tr>

</th>
<td>IJB 427
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>D major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>5 movements:
<ol><li>Chorus: O ewiges Feuer, o Ursprung der Liebe
</li><li>Recitativo (Tenor): Herr, unsre Herzen halten dir
</li><li>Aria (Alto): Wohl euch, ihr auserwählten Seelen
</li><li>Recitativo (Bass): Erwählt sich die heilgen Hütten
</li><li>Chorus: Friede über Israel
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1726-27 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>

<td>1727-06-01 in Leipzig
</td></tr>

<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>

</td></tr>

<ul><li>Cantatas, BWV 221–224
</li></ul>
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td style="background-color: #e6f0f5">
<ul><li> BWV 221: <i>Wer sucht die Pracht, wer wünscht den Glanz</i> (composer unknown}
</li><li> BWV 222: <i>Mein Odem ist schwach</i> (by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Ernst" title="Category:Bach, Johann Ernst">Johann Ernst Bach</a>)
</li><li> BWV 223: <i>Meine Seele soll Gott loben</i>
</li><li> BWV 224: <i>Reisst euch los, bekränkte Sinnen</i> (by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Carl_Philipp_Emanuel" title="Category:Bach, Carl Philipp Emanuel">Carl Philipp Emanuel Bach</a>?)
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
</td></tr></table>
